<div id="review_710176897" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/710176897" />
    <a title="Becky" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/966742-becky"><img alt="Becky" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1234398782p2/966742.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/710176897?book_show_action=true">Sep 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Becky" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Becky" href="/user/show/966742-becky">Becky</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/966742-becky?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/966742-becky?shelf=printz-award-winners-and-honorees">printz-award-winners-and-honorees</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/966742-becky?shelf=dystopia-and-or-post-apocalypse">dystopia-and-or-post-apocalypse</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/966742-becky?shelf=fya-book-club">fya-book-club</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer710176897" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6763982728737595166">So okay, I had no idea what <i>Maggot Moon</i> was about before I started reading it. I just knew people liked it a lot. So as I was reading I kept wondering how much of it was based on real history. I mean, it certainly sounds like Standish is living in a Soviet occupied country. But I was reading it in the middle of the woods on a mountain with no data service for miles, so I just had to finish the book instead. And while it becomes apparent that the Motherland is not exactly the Soviet Union (the pr</span>
  <span id="freeText6763982728737595166" style="display:none">So okay, I had no idea what <i>Maggot Moon</i> was about before I started reading it. I just knew people liked it a lot. So as I was reading I kept wondering how much of it was based on real history. I mean, it certainly sounds like Standish is living in a Soviet occupied country. But I was reading it in the middle of the woods on a mountain with no data service for miles, so I just had to finish the book instead. And while it becomes apparent that the Motherland is not exactly the Soviet Union (the president is female, for one), it's so close I think this book really does something for the genre. I mean, dystopic fiction got its start because lots of that crazy totalitarian stuff was really happening in communist and fascist countries. It <i>still</i> happens in places like North Korea, but I don't think people really think of it that way. They see this new crop of YA dystopia as futuristic speculation, as cautionary tales maybe, as alarmist even. But Sally Gardner takes her story and sets in the past, in a place so startlingly recognizable you can't ignore it. These terrible things, they REALLY HAPPEN.<br /><br />But that's not all! Standish is such a great character. He is well-drawn, intelligent and brave and also dyslexic. The story is crafted in this fantastic loop, and it's complemented by these disturbing illustrations of a fly's life cycle, including the rat whose poisoned corpse becomes the home for growing maggots. <br /><br />This is some serious, complex storytelling. You should read it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6763982728737595166" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_933547459" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/933547459" />
    <a title="Jenne" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/26259-jenne"><img alt="Jenne" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1173836583p2/26259.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/933547459?book_show_action=true">May 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenne" href="/user/show/26259-jenne">Jenne</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26259-jenne?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26259-jenne?shelf=sf">sf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26259-jenne?shelf=fifty-fifty-me-2014">fifty-fifty-me-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer933547459" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17492361243104248737">I don't quite know how to describe why I loved this book so much. It's a very simple story when you look back on it (which I've been doing a lot of since I read it) but it takes a while to get your bearings while you're reading it. There's also a slight feeling of Daniel Pinkwater, like if Baconburg was taken over by the SS, and I adore Daniel Pinkwater. And the ending! The ending was exactly right. <br/>I've never read anything by Sally Gardner before, but her writing is so tightly crafted, so assur</span>
  <span id="freeText17492361243104248737" style="display:none">I don't quite know how to describe why I loved this book so much. It's a very simple story when you look back on it (which I've been doing a lot of since I read it) but it takes a while to get your bearings while you're reading it. There's also a slight feeling of Daniel Pinkwater, like if Baconburg was taken over by the SS, and I adore Daniel Pinkwater. And the ending! The ending was exactly right. <br />I've never read anything by Sally Gardner before, but her writing is so tightly crafted, so assured, that you don't realize till later that you aren't actually reading the diary of a highly imaginative, dyslexic teenager who is living through a horrific totalitarian nightmare. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17492361243104248737" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_958092831" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/958092831" />
    <a title="André Caniato" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9074347-andr-caniato"><img alt="André Caniato" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1493655245p2/9074347.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/958092831?book_show_action=true">Jan 17, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="André Caniato" class="user" itemprop="url" name="André Caniato" href="/user/show/9074347-andr-caniato">André Caniato</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781471400063" href="/book/show/18710161-maggot-moon">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer958092831" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7776124569925326582"><i>Maggot Moon</i> is different from anything I've read before. I don't even know how to label it. Historical dystopia, maybe? I'm not sure 'alternate history' does it, although it <i>is</i> an alternate history of some sort, set in an universe which took obvious inspiration from Nazi Germany and Orwell's 1984. It's a beautiful, touching story—as disturbing as it is moving, with compelling characters and unique prose.</span>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

<div id="review_2059693494" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2059693494" />
    <a title="Irina Cebanu" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/52673821-irina-cebanu"><img alt="Irina Cebanu" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583614880p2/52673821.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2059693494?book_show_action=true">Aug 16, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Irina Cebanu" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Irina Cebanu" href="/user/show/52673821-irina-cebanu">Irina Cebanu</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9786069351055" href="/book/show/22181716-cele-trei-fe-e-ale-lunii">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2059693494" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5697090551879126479">I know I wouldn't be able to put it in beautiful words, but I felt like I had to write a review, because I liked it a lot. To put it simply, it is one of the best books I've ever read. The style of writing is not really intricate, which I consider to be wonderful, since complex writings often are an impediment to the story itself (Generally, it seems to me that the authors who prefer writing intricately, using complex words and unusual syntax are focused more on the style of the writing than the</span>
  <span id="freeText5697090551879126479" style="display:none">I know I wouldn't be able to put it in beautiful words, but I felt like I had to write a review, because I liked it a lot. To put it simply, it is one of the best books I've ever read. The style of writing is not really intricate, which I consider to be wonderful, since complex writings often are an impediment to the story itself (Generally, it seems to me that the authors who prefer writing intricately, using complex words and unusual syntax are focused more on the style of the writing than the story itself and I guess that's what they think the readers would like, but I for one find this obnoxious). The story is captivating till the last moment. It is also an example of an exceptionally good translation into Romanian. I wholeheartedly recommend it, especially to those who like books with sci-fi elements, about oppressive government and about ordinary people being heroes.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5697090551879126479" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('JhkcY8Mf/HDDzCJn50vJqFP2j8Iji4UMb/J9zZ7M7v+fT0jqLo43sVzXyIO5fXv4gqZLtvHN7U0jo+OWxv0b3Q==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('5SS9d2Sa8SYEsTPzKr+dDskIpOmuJjXXpZegNNgzdmZccun+iQs655uq2Rd0iS9eGFhgnXxgXZbpxj5vgAKDRA==')})
  }

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/145946.Sally_Gardner">About Sally Gardner</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer2449164405518144479">Sally Gardner grew up and still lives in London. Being dyslexic, she did not learn to read or write until she was fourteen and had been thrown out of several schools, labeled unteachable, and sent to a school for maladjusted children. Despite this, she gained a degree with highest honors at a leading London art college, followed by a scholarship to a theater school, and then went on to become a ve</span>
  <span id="freeText2449164405518144479" style="display:none">Sally Gardner grew up and still lives in London. Being dyslexic, she did not learn to read or write until she was fourteen and had been thrown out of several schools, labeled unteachable, and sent to a school for maladjusted children. Despite this, she gained a degree with highest honors at a leading London art college, followed by a scholarship to a theater school, and then went on to become a very successful costume designer, working on some notable productions. <br /><br />After the births of twin daughters and a son, she started first to illustrate and then to write picture books and chapter books, usually with fairytale- or otherwise magical subject matter. She has been called 'an idiosyncratic genius' by London’s Sunday Times.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2449164405518144479" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
